NTR_lost_state_control = {
	set_state_flag = NTR_state_control_lost_flag
	set_demilitarized_zone = yes
	add_state_modifier = {
		modifier = {
			local_building_slots_factor = -1
			local_factories = -1
			local_resources = -1
		}
	}
}

NTR_lost_state_control_with_tooltip = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_lost_state_control_tooltip
	hidden_effect = { NTR_lost_state_control = yes }
}

NTR_restore_state_control = {
	clr_state_flag = NTR_state_control_lost_flag
	set_demilitarized_zone = no
	add_state_modifier = {
		modifier = {
			local_building_slots_factor = 1
			local_factories = 1
			local_resources = 1
		}
	}
}

NTR_restore_state_control_with_tooltip = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_restore_state_control_tooltip
	hidden_effect = { NTR_restore_state_control = yes }
}

population_calculator_multifunctional = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { population_var > 0 } # check for overflow
		}
		
		divide_variable = { population_var = ROOT.divider }
		
		#print_variables = {
		#	file = check_effect
		#	text = Population_pre
		#	append = yes
		#	var_list = {
		#		population_var
		#		ROOT.divider
		#		ROOT.randomizer
		#		ROOT.rounder
		#	}
		#}
		
		set_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = population_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = ROOT.randomizer }
		multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = random }
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = -1 }
			}
			50 = {
				# nothing
			}
		}
		
		add_to_variable = { population_var = population_variation_temp_var }
		
		divide_variable = { population_var = ROOT.rounder }
		round_variable = population_var
		multiply_variable = { population_var = ROOT.rounder }
		
		#print_variables = {
		#	file = check_effect
		#	text = Population_post
		#	append = yes
		#	var_list = {
		#		population_var
		#		population_variation_temp_var
		#	}
		#}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { population_var = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { population_var = ROOT.divider }
		
		set_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = population_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = ROOT.randomizer }
		multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = random }
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { population_variation_temp_var = -1 }
			}
			50 = {
				# nothing
			}
		}
		
		add_to_variable = { population_var = population_variation_temp_var }
		multiply_variable = { population_var = 1000 }
	}
}

population_calculator_cleaner = {
	clear_variable = divider
	clear_variable = randomizer
	clear_variable = rounder
}

population_clr_junk = {
	clear_variable = population_var
	clear_variable = population_sum
}

population_calculation_for_sum = {

	add_manpower = population_var
	
	#print_variables = {

	#		population_var

	#	}
	#}
}

calculate_NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = modern_society
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # >= outdated
			check_variable = {
				var = EaW_society_development_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = 5
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = outdated_industry
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.3 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.25 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # >= industrializing
			check_variable = {
				var = EaW_society_development_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = 4
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = pre_industrial_society
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = pre_industrial_society1
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = -0.45 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = pre_industrial_society2
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.4 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.35 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # >= agrarian
			check_variable = {
				var = EaW_society_development_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = 3
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = agrarian_society
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.8 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = agrarian_society2
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.75 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = agrarian_society3
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.7 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = agrarian_society4
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.65 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = agrarian_society5
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.6 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.55 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { # >= communal
			check_variable = {
				var = EaW_society_development_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = 2
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = communal_society2
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.85 }
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = NTR_millennial_experience
						has_completed_focus = NTR_modernize_communes
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = NTR_autonomous_communes
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.45 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.675 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.9 }
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # detached or tribal
		set_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 1 }
	}
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = NTR_average_country_agricultural_production_var }
	multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = NTR_current_year_agricultural_support_var }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_decision = NTR_help_from_friends
				has_decision = NTR_buy_food
				has_decision = NTR_help_from_comrades
			}
		}
		
		divide_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 2 }
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = tech_pony_misc
		}
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var = 0.75 }
	}
}

calculate_NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffs = {
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_stability_debuff_var = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { NTR_famine_stability_debuff_var = modifier@stability_factor }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_stability_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_buildings_speed_debuff_var = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { NTR_famine_buildings_speed_debuff_var = modifier@production_speed_buildings_factor }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_buildings_speed_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_monthly_population_debuff_var = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { NTR_famine_monthly_population_debuff_var = modifier@monthly_population }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_monthly_population_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_army_org_debuff_var = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { NTR_famine_army_org_debuff_var = modifier@army_org_factor }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_army_org_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_army_morale_factor_debuff_var = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { NTR_famine_army_morale_factor_debuff_var = modifier@army_morale_factor }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_army_morale_factor_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	set_variable = { NTR_famine_training_time_army_factor_debuff_var = -1 }
	subtract_from_variable = { NTR_famine_training_time_army_factor_debuff_var = modifier@training_time_army_factor }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_famine_training_time_army_factor_debuff_var = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier_debuffer_temp_var }
	
	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_famine_dynamic_modifier }
}

add_NTR_traditionalism_influence_dynamic_modifier_effects = {
	set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_enemy_justify_war_goal_time_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_united_northern_front_flag
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = -0.4 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = -1 }
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = -0.8 }
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_war_support_factor_var = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_conscription_factor_var = -1 }
			set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = -1 }
			
			multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_war_support_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_conscription_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_war_support_factor_var = -0.2 }
		
		multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_war_support_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
	}
	
	multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
}

add_NTR_communist_partisans_dynamic_modifier_effects = {
	set_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_political_power_factor_var = -1 }
	set_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_stability_factor_var = -0.8 }
	set_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_war_support_factor_var = -0.5 }
	set_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_conscription_factor_var = -1 }
	set_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = -1 }
	
	multiply_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_political_power_factor_var = party_popularity@communism }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@communism }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_war_support_factor_var = party_popularity@communism }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_conscription_factor_var = party_popularity@communism }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@communism }
}

add_NTR_harmonic_tribes_dynamic_modifier_effects = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NTR_united_northern_front_flag
		}
		
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_political_power_factor_var = -0.5 }
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_stability_factor_var = -0.4 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_political_power_factor_var = -1 }
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_stability_factor_var = -0.8 }
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_war_support_factor_var = -0.5 }
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_conscription_factor_var = -1 }
		set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = -1 }
		
		multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_war_support_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
		multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_conscription_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
		multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_offensive_war_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
	}
	
	multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_political_power_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
	multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
}

NTR_randomise_political_path = {
	random_list = {
		20 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA }
		20 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE }
		15 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH }
		15 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION }
		15 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS }
		15 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS }
	}
}

NTR_clr_advisors_help_flags = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA }
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE }
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH }
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION }
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS }
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS
	}
	else = {
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
	}
}

calculate_NTR_unite_the_tribes_positive_drift = {
	set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var = random } # 0-1
	divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var = 4 } # max 0.25
	
	set_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = 0.75 }
	
	random_list = {
		50 = { # (0.5 ~ 0.75)
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var }
		}
		50 = { # (0.75 ~ 1)
			add_to_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var }
		}
	}
}

calculate_NTR_unite_the_tribes_negative_drift = {
	set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var = random } # 0-1
	divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var = 10 } # max 0.1
	
	set_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = -0.25 }
	
	random_list = {
		50 = { # (-0.35 ~ -0.25)
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var }
		}
		50 = { # (-0.25 ~ -0.15)
			add_to_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_drift_randomizer_temp_var }
		}
	}
}

NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_ROOT_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = agrarian_society2 }
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = agrarian_society
			add_idea = agrarian_society2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = agrarian_society3 }
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = agrarian_society2
			add_idea = agrarian_society3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = agrarian_society4 }
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = agrarian_society3
			add_idea = agrarian_society4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = agrarian_society5 }
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = agrarian_society4
			add_idea = agrarian_society5
		}
	}
	else = {
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = agrarian_society5
			add_idea = agrarian_society6
		}
	}
}

NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_idea = modern_society }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = owned_states
						
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_political_power = -35
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -40
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				check_variable = {
					var = EaW_society_development_var
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = owned_states
						
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -60
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				check_variable = {
					var = EaW_society_development_var
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = owned_states
						
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_political_power = -65
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -80
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

NTR_griffon_race_technologies_show_complete_effect_for_127_days = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_effects_tooltip
	
	hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_cooldown
			value = 1
			days = 127
		}
		
		country_event = Ntribes.991
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.991 started"
	}
}

		country_event = Ntribes.990
	}
}

NTR_save_random_state_as_target_for_complex = {
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
				building = industrial_complex
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				
				NOT = {
					ROOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		
		add_building_construction = {
			type = industrial_complex
			level = 1
			instant_build = yes
		}
		
		set_variable = { PREV.NTR_state_with_one_bonus_complex = THIS }
	}
}

NTR_save_random_state_as_target_for_dockyard = { #???
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_controlled_by = PREV
				is_coastal = yes
			}
			
			NOT = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					
					dockyard > 0
					
					free_building_slots = {
						building = dockyard
						size > 2
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_coastal = yes
				
				free_building_slots = {
					building = dockyard
					size > 2
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			set_variable = { PREV.NTR_state_with_one_bonus_dockyard = THIS }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = naval_effort_built }
			
			any_owned_state = {
				is_controlled_by = PREV
				
				dockyard > 0
				
				free_building_slots = {
					building = dockyard
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				dockyard > 0
				
				free_building_slots = {
					building = dockyard
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			set_variable = { PREV.NTR_state_with_one_bonus_dockyard = THIS }
		}
	}
}

add_NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 0 }
		}
		
		NTR = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			
			clear_variable = NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 1 }
		}
		
		NTR = {
			set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.05 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild } }
				}
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 2 }
		}
		
		NTR = {
			set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.1 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild } }
				}
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		NTR = {
			set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.15 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild } }
				}
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
	}
}

factories_calculation = { # Tribute shit #NotInUse
	set_temp_variable = { industrial_complexes_check = industrial_complex_level }
	divide_temp_variable = { industrial_complexes_check = 2 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = industrial_complexes_check
				compare = not_equals
				value = add_industrial_complexes
			}
		}
		
		var:to_country = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = add_industrial_complexes
			}
		}
		
		multiply_variable = { add_industrial_complexes = -1 }
		
		ROOT = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = add_industrial_complexes
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { add_industrial_complexes = industrial_complexes_check }
		multiply_variable = { add_industrial_complexes = -1 }
		
		var:to_country = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = add_industrial_complexes
			}
		}
		
		multiply_variable = { add_industrial_complexes = -1 }
		
		ROOT = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = add_industrial_complexes
			}
		}
	}
	
	set_temp_variable = { arms_factories_check = arms_factory_level }
	divide_temp_variable = { arms_factories_check = 2 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = arms_factories_check
				compare = not_equals
				value = add_arms_factories
			}
		}
		
		var:to_country = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = add_arms_factories
			}
		}
		
		multiply_variable = { add_arms_factories = -1 }
		
		ROOT = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = add_arms_factories
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { add_arms_factories = arms_factories_check }
		multiply_variable = { add_arms_factories = -1 }
		
		var:to_country = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = add_arms_factories
			}
		}
		
		multiply_variable = { add_arms_factories = -1 }
		
		ROOT = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = add_arms_factories
			}
		}
	}
}

calculate_NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_ai_behavior = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			communism > 0
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				communism < 0.05
			}
			
			activate_decision = NTR_the_last_assault_on_frostbell
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_breaking_the_tribal_council
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							democratic > 0.33
						}
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								communism < 0.15
								
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								neutrality < 0.15
								
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									communism > 0.15
									neutrality > 0.15
									
									NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_play_the_tribal_council_and_the_communists_against_each_other_cooldown_flag }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_play_the_tribal_council_and_the_communists_against_each_other
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										democratic > 0.5
									}
									
									if = {
										limit = {
											check_variable = { party_popularity@communism < party_popularity@neutrality }
										}
										
										if = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
											}
											
											activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
										}
										else = {
											activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
										}
									}
									else = {
										if = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task_cooldown_flag }
											}
											
											activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
										}
										else = {
											activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
										}
									}
								}
								else = {
									activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
							}
							else = {
								activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						democratic > 0.5
						
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
				}
				else = {
					activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			neutrality > 0
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				neutrality < 0.05
			}
			
			activate_decision = NTR_breaking_the_tribal_council
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task_cooldown_flag }
				}
				
				activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
			}
			else = {
				activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
			}
		}
	}
}

calculate_NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_ai_behavior = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			communism > 0
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				communism < 0.05
			}
			
			activate_decision = NTR_the_last_assault_on_frostbell
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					democratic > 0
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						democratic < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_do_away_with_the_snowflakes
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							neutrality > 0.33
						}
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								communism < 0.15
								
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								democratic < 0.15
								
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									communism > 0.15
									democratic > 0.15
									
									NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_unite_under_one_banner_by_force_or_diplomacy_cooldown_flag }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_unite_under_one_banner_by_force_or_diplomacy
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										neutrality > 0.5
									}
									
									if = {
										limit = {
											check_variable = { party_popularity@communism < party_popularity@democratic }
										}
										
										if = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
											}
											
											activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
										}
										else = {
											activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
										}
									}
									else = {
										if = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters_cooldown_flag }
											}
											
											activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
										}
										else = {
											activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
										}
									}
								}
								else = {
									activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_millennial_traditions_cooldown_flag }
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
							}
							else = {
								activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality > 0.5
						
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists_cooldown_flag }
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
				}
				else = {
					activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			democratic > 0
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				democratic < 0.05
			}
			
			activate_decision = NTR_do_away_with_the_snowflakes
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters_cooldown_flag }
				}
				
				activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
			}
			else = {
				activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
			}
		}
	}
}

NTR_add_morker_river_and_vastmush_river_bunkers = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = normal } }
		563 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 2075 id = 6424 id = 566 }
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
				province = 11510
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 4
				instant_build = yes
				province = 1318
			}
		}
		573 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 7348 id = 2090 id = 12101 }
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 4
				instant_build = yes
				province = 8962
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 11480 id = 11591 }
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
				province = 7322
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_1 } }
			563 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 2075 id = 6424 id = 566 id = 11510 id = 1318 }
				}
			}
			573 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 7348 id = 8962 id = 2090 id = 11480 id = 7322 id = 11591 id = 12101 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_2 } }
			563 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 2075 id = 6424 id = 566 id = 1318 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_province_building_level = {
								building = bunker
								level < 1 # 1-...
								province = { id = 11510 }
							}
						}
					}
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
						province = 11510

									type = bunker
									level = 3

								}

								level = 2
								instant_build = yes
								province = { id = 6523 id = 11578 }

							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
							province = { id = 6523 id = 11578 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

NTR_add_moonrise_hills_bunkers = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = normal } }
		add_building_construction = {
			type = bunker
			level = 3
			instant_build = yes
			province = 477
		}
		add_building_construction = {
			type = bunker

			instant_build = yes
			province = { id = 3459 id = 11578 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_1 } }

NTR_add_braunles_hills_bunkers = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = normal } }
		add_building_construction = {
			type = bunker
			level = 3
			instant_build = yes
			province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
		}
		add_building_construction = {
			type = bunker
			level = 4
			instant_build = yes
			province = { id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 }
		}
		add_building_construction = {
			type = bunker
			level = 5
			instant_build = yes
			province = 1737
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_1 } }
			set_building_level = {
				type = bunker
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 id = 1737 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_2 } }
			set_building_level = {
				type = bunker
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 id = 1737 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_3 } }
			set_building_level = {
				type = bunker
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 id = 1737 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_4 } }
			set_building_level = {
				type = bunker
				level = 4
				instant_build = yes
				province = { id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 id = 1737 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_province_building_level = {
							building = bunker
							level < 1 # 1-...
							province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = level_5 } }
			set_building_level = {
				type = bunker
				level = 5
				instant_build = yes
				province = 1737
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_province_building_level = {
							building = bunker
							level < 1 # 1-...
							province = { id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 }

					}
				}
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 }

			}
			else = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 1943 id = 2074 id = 12890 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_province_building_level = {
							building = bunker
							level < 1 # 1-...

					}
				}
				if = {

								building = bunker
								level < 2 # 2-...

						}
					}
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 5
						instant_build = yes
						province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 4
						instant_build = yes
						province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = bunker
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
					province = { id = 10911 id = 13067 }
				}
			}
		}

add_NTR_vedinian_line_bunkers = {
	542 = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { # check for defense breakthrough
					any_province_building_level = {
						building = bunker
						level < 11
						province = {
							id = 4874
							id = 12117
							id = 6575
							id = 6541
							id = 1808
							id = 361
							id = 3578
							limit_to_border = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			NTR_add_borasland_river_bunkers = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_2_border_bunkers_with_maximum_fort_level_rule = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { # check for defense breakthrough
				542 = {
					any_province_building_level = {
						building = bunker
						level < 11

					}

		}

	}
}

add_NTR_southern_line_bunkers = {
	567 = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = maximum_fort_level option = normal } }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_border = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_4_border_bunkers_with_maximum_fort_level_rule = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_3_border_bunkers_with_maximum_fort_level_rule = yes
		}
	}
